/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_AddMileage]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_AddMileage]
	@game		tinyint,
	@createid	int,
	@account		varchar(20),
	@uid		int,
	@cid		int,
	@ip		varchar(15)
--WITH ENCRYPTION
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @err int
DECLARE @err0 int
DECLARE @err1 int
DECLARE @err2 int
DECLARE @tmp_itemid int
DECLARE @tmp_amount int
DECLARE @tmp_max_amount int
DECLARE @itemname varchar(100)
DECLARE @itemid varchar(50)
DECLARE @amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @point int
DECLARE @price smallmoney
DECLARE @t_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_itemid varchar(50)

-- 아이템 확인
select @err0=count(*) from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 1
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 1  -- 아이템 번호 에러
end
-- 계정 확인
if @game=0
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ichman.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @game=1
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ponpon.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 4
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 4  -- 계정 에러
end

if @err0>0
begin
	-- 상품 획득 자료
	select @itemid=ItemPrototypeID, @itemname=ItemName, @point=point, @price=price, @amount=amount, @max_amount=max_amount from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
	
	set @t_itemid=@itemid
	set @t_amount=@amount
	set @t_max_amount=@max_amount
	
	-- 아이템 추가전 임시인벤 확인 (최대 20개가 한계)
	if @game=0
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @game=1
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @err0>0
	begin
		select @err=2
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount, @itemid as itemid
		return 2 -- 아이템 구매 수량이 최대치 니 게임에 먼저 접속해라.
	end
	if @err0=0
	begin
		-- 신화점수 차감
		DECLARE @RESULT int

		exec  @RESULT = Pay_Gamemyth.dbo.spPayAuthUID_Web @account, @ip, @point
		if @RESULT > 0
		begin
			select @RESULT as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid

			return @RESULT
		end

		-- 아이템 번호 정리
		
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		if @err0=0 -- 1개
		begin	
			set @tmp_amount = @amount
			set @tmp_max_amount = @max_amount
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				if @game=0
				begin
					-- 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					-- 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			end
			
			-- 아이템 추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			-- 판매기록 입력
			exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
			select @err=0
			select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid
			return 0
		end
		
		select @itemid = @t_itemid
		select @amount = @t_amount
		select @max_amount = @t_max_amount
		--set @tmp_itemid=@itemid
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)

		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		
		while @err0>0 -- 다수
		begin
			select @tmp_itemid = left(@itemid,@err0-1)
			select @itemid = substring(@itemid,
@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
		
			select @tmp_amount = left(@amount,@err1-1)
			select @tmp_max_amount = left(@max_amount,@err2-1)
			select @amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
			select @max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
		
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
		
				-- 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
			end
			-- 아이템추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
			select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
			select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
			
			if @err0=0
			begin
				select @tmp_itemid = substring(@itemid,@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
				select @tmp_amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
				select @tmp_max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
				while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
				begin
					select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			
					-- 아이템 추가
					if @game=0
					begin
						insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
					if @game=1
					begin
						insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
				end
				-- 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
			end
		end
		
		exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @t_itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
		select @err=0
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
		, @itemid as itemid
		return 0
	end
end
		
select @err as err
return @err

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_BuyItemAdd]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_BuyItemAdd]
	@game		tinyint,
	@createid	int,
	@account		varchar(20),
	@uid		int,
	@cid		int,
	@ip		varchar(15)
--WITH ENCRYPTION
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @err int
DECLARE @err0 int
DECLARE @err1 int
DECLARE @err2 int
DECLARE @tmp_itemid int
DECLARE @tmp_amount int
DECLARE @tmp_max_amount int
DECLARE @itemname varchar(100)
DECLARE @itemid varchar(50)
DECLARE @amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @point int
DECLARE @price smallmoney
DECLARE @t_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_itemid varchar(50)

--道具確認 : 아이템 확인
select @err0=count(*) from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 1
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 1  --道具編號錯誤 ? 아이템 번호 에러
end
--帳號確認 ? 계정 확인
if @game=0
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ichman.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @game=1
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ponpon.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 4
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 4  --帳號錯誤 ? 계정 에러
end

if @err0>0
begin
	--取得商品資訊 ? 상품 획득 자료
	select @itemid=ItemPrototypeID, @itemname=ItemName, @point=point, @price=price, @amount=amount, @max_amount=max_amount from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
	
	set @t_itemid=@itemid
	set @t_amount=@amount
	set @t_max_amount=@max_amount
	
	--新增前先確認是否有未領道具達20件 ? 아이템 추가전 임시인벤 확인 (최대 20개가 한계)
	if @game=0
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @game=1
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @err0>0
	begin
		select @err=2
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount, @itemid as itemid
		return 2 --道具購買數量超過最大?，請先進入遊?領取 ? 아이템 구매 수량이 최대치 니 게임에 먼저 접속해라.
	end
	if @err0=0
	begin
		--?神話點數 ? 신화점수 차감
		DECLARE @RESULT int

		exec  @RESULT = Pay_Gamemyth.dbo.spPayAuthUID_Web @account, @ip, @point
		if @RESULT > 0
		begin
			select @RESULT as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid

			return @RESULT
		end

		--道具編號整理 ? 아이템 번호 정리
		
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		if @err0=0 --單筆 ? 1개
		begin	
			set @tmp_amount = @amount
			set @tmp_max_amount = @max_amount
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				if @game=0
				begin
					--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			end
			
			--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			--記錄寫入 ? 판매기록 입력
			exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
			select @err=0
			select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid
			return 0
		end
		
		select @itemid = @t_itemid
		select @amount = @t_amount
		select @max_amount = @t_max_amount
		--set @tmp_itemid=@itemid
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)

		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		
		while @err0>0 --多筆 - 다수
		begin
			select @tmp_itemid = left(@itemid,@err0-1)
			select @itemid = substring(@itemid,
@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
		
			select @tmp_amount = left(@amount,@err1-1)
			select @tmp_max_amount = left(@max_amount,@err2-1)
			select @amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
			select @max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
		
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
		
				--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
			end
			--新增道具 - 아이템추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
			select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
			select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
			
			if @err0=0
			begin
				select @tmp_itemid = substring(@itemid,@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
				select @tmp_amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
				select @tmp_max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
				while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
				begin
					select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			
					--新增道具 아이템 추가
					if @game=0
					begin
						insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
					if @game=1
					begin
						insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
				end
				--新增道具 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ichman.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Ponpon.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
			end
		end
		
		exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @t_itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
		select @err=0
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
		, @itemid as itemid
		return 0
	end
end
		
select @err as err
return @err

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_BuyItemAdd_Test]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_BuyItemAdd_Test]
	@game		tinyint,
	@createid	int,
	@account		varchar(20),
	@uid		int,
	@cid		int,
	@ip		varchar(15)
--WITH ENCRYPTION
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @err int
DECLARE @err0 int
DECLARE @err1 int
DECLARE @err2 int
DECLARE @tmp_itemid int
DECLARE @tmp_amount int
DECLARE @tmp_max_amount int
DECLARE @itemname varchar(100)
DECLARE @itemid varchar(50)
DECLARE @amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @point int
DECLARE @price smallmoney
DECLARE @t_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_max_amount varchar(50)
DECLARE @t_itemid varchar(50)

--道具確認 : 아이템 확인
select @err0=count(*) from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 1
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 1  --道具編號錯誤 ? 아이템 번호 에러
end
--帳號確認 ? 계정 확인
if @game=0
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Test.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @game=1
begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Test.dbo.vuserinfo where uid=@uid and cid = @cid
end
if @err0=0
begin
	select @err = 4
	select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
	, @itemid as itemid
	return 4  --帳號錯誤 ? 계정 에러
end

if @err0>0
begin
	--取得商品資訊 ? 상품 획득 자료
	select @itemid=ItemPrototypeID, @itemname=ItemName, @point=point, @price=price, @amount=amount, @max_amount=max_amount from SellItem where CreateID = @createid
	
	set @t_itemid=@itemid
	set @t_amount=@amount
	set @t_max_amount=@max_amount
	
	--新增前先確認是否有未領道具達20件 ? 아이템 추가전 임시인벤 확인 (최대 20개가 한계)
	if @game=0
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @game=1
	begin
	select @err0=count(*) from ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo where cid=@cid and (itemuid=0 or itemuid=-1)
	end
	if @err0>0
	begin
		select @err=2
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount, @itemid as itemid
		return 2 --道具購買數量超過最大?，請先進入遊?領取 ? 아이템 구매 수량이 최대치 니 게임에 먼저 접속해라.
	end
	if @err0=0
	begin
		--?神話點數 ? 신화점수 차감
		DECLARE @RESULT int

		exec  @RESULT = Pay_Gamemyth.dbo.spPayAuthUID_Web @account, @ip, @point
		if @RESULT > 0
		begin
			select @RESULT as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid

			return @RESULT
		end

		--道具編號整理 ? 아이템 번호 정리
		
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		if @err0=0 --單筆 ? 1개
		begin	
			set @tmp_amount = @amount
			set @tmp_max_amount = @max_amount
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				if @game=0
				begin
					--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			end
			
			--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			--記錄寫入 ? 판매기록 입력
			exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
			select @err=0
			select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
			, @itemid as itemid
			return 0
		end
		
		select @itemid = @t_itemid
		select @amount = @t_amount
		select @max_amount = @t_max_amount
		--set @tmp_itemid=@itemid
		select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)

		select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
		select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
		
		while @err0>0 --多筆 - 다수
		begin
			select @tmp_itemid = left(@itemid,@err0-1)
			select @itemid = substring(@itemid,
@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
		
			select @tmp_amount = left(@amount,@err1-1)
			select @tmp_max_amount = left(@max_amount,@err2-1)
			select @amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
			select @max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
		
			while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
			begin
				select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
		
				--新增道具 ? 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
				end
			end
			--新增道具 - 아이템추가
			if @game=0
			begin
				insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			if @game=1
			begin
				insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
				(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
				values
				(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
			end
			select @err0=charindex('|', @itemid)
			select @err1=charindex('|', @amount)
			select @err2=charindex('|', @max_amount)
			
			if @err0=0
			begin
				select @tmp_itemid = substring(@itemid,@err0+1, len(@itemid)-@err0)
				select @tmp_amount = substring(@amount,@err2+1, len(@amount)-@err1)
				select @tmp_max_amount = substring(@max_amount,@err2+1, len(@max_amount)-@err2)
				while @tmp_amount>@tmp_max_amount
				begin
					select @tmp_amount=@tmp_amount-@tmp_max_amount
			
					--新增道具 아이템 추가
					if @game=0
					begin
						insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
					if @game=1
					begin
						insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
						(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
						values
						(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_max_amount)
					end
				end
				--新增道具 아이템 추가
				if @game=0
				begin
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
				if @game=1
				begin
					insert into ROW_Test.dbo.TblWebItemInfo 
					(uid, cid,ItemPrototypeID, amount)
					values
					(@uid, @cid, @tmp_itemid, @tmp_amount)
				end
			end
		end
		
		exec sp_SellLog @createid, @uid, @cid, @t_itemid, @itemname, @t_amount, @point, @price, @ip
		select @err=0
		select @err as err, @err0 as err0, @err1 as err1, @err2 as err2, @tmp_amount as tmp_amount, @tmp_max_amount as tmp_max_amount
		, @itemid as itemid
		return 0
	end
end
		
select @err as err
return @err

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_decrypt]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create  PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_decrypt](@objectname varchar(50))
AS
begin
set nocount on
--CSDN：j9988 copyright:2004.07.15 
--V3.2 
--破解字?不受限制，适用于SQLSERVER2000存??程，函?，??，触?器
--修正上一版"??触?器"不能正确解密??
--??有?，?E_MAIL：CSDNj9988@tom.com
begin tran
declare @objectname1 varchar(100),@orgvarbin varbinary(8000)
declare @sql1 nvarchar(4000),@sql2 varchar(8000),@sql3 nvarchar(4000),@sql4 nvarchar(4000)
DECLARE  @OrigSpText1 nvarchar(4000),  @OrigSpText2 nvarchar(4000) , @OrigSpText3 nvarchar(4000), @resultsp nvarchar(4000)
declare  @i int,@status int,@type varchar(10),@parentid int
declare @colid int,@n int,@q int,@j int,@k int,@encrypted int,@number int
select @type=xtype,@parentid=parent_obj from sysobjects where id=object_id(@objectname)
create table  #temp(number int,colid int,ctext varbinary(8000),encrypted int,status int)
insert #temp SELECT number,colid,ctext,encrypted,status FROM syscomments  WHERE id = object_id(@objectname)
select @number=max(number) from #temp
set @k=0
while @k<=@number 
begin
if exists(select 1 from syscomments where id=object_id(@objectname) and number=@k)
begin
if @type='P'
set @sql1=(case when @number>1 then 'ALTER PROCEDURE '+ @objectname +';'+rtrim(@k)+' WITH ENCRYPTION AS '
                          else 'ALTER PROCEDURE '+ @objectname+' WITH ENCRYPTION AS '
                          end)
if @type='TR'
begin
declare @parent_obj varchar(255),@tr_parent_xtype varchar(10)
select @parent_obj=parent_obj from sysobjects where id=object_id(@objectname)
select @tr_parent_xtype=xtype from sysobjects where id=@parent_obj
if @tr_parent_xtype='V'
begin
set @sql1='ALTER TRIGGER '+@objectname+' ON '+OBJECT_NAME(@parentid)+' WITH ENCRYPTION INSTERD OF INSERT AS PRINT 1 '
end
else
begin
set @sql1='ALTER TRIGGER '+@objectname+' ON '+OBJECT_NAME(@parentid)+' WITH ENCRYPTION FOR INSERT AS PRINT 1 '
end
end
if @type='FN' or @type='TF' or @type='IF'
set @sql1=(case @type when 'TF' then 
'ALTER FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns @b table(a varchar(10)) with encryption as begin insert @b select @a return end '
when 'FN' then
'ALTER FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns char(1) with encryption as begin return @a end'
when 'IF' then
'ALTER FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns table with encryption as return select @a as a'
end)
if @type='V'
set @sql1='ALTER VIEW '+@objectname+' WITH ENCRYPTION AS SELECT 1 as f'
set @q=len(@sql1)
set @sql1=@sql1+REPLICATE('-',4000-@q)
select @sql2=REPLICATE('-',8000)
set @sql3='exec(@sql1'
select @colid=max(colid) from #temp where number=@k 
set @n=1
while @n<=CEILING(1.0*(@colid-1)/2) and len(@sql3)<=3996
begin 
set @sql3=@sql3+'+@'
set @n=@n+1
end
set @sql3=@sql3+')'
exec sp_executesql @sql3,N'@sql1 nvarchar(4000),@ varchar(8000)',@sql1=@sql1,@=@sql2
end
set @k=@k+1
end
set @k=0
while @k<=@number 
begin
if exists(select 1 from syscomments where id=object_id(@objectname) and number=@k)
begin
select @colid=max(colid) from #temp where number=@k 
set @n=1
while @n<=@colid
begin
select @OrigSpText1=ctext,@encrypted=encrypted,@status=status FROM #temp  WHERE colid=@n and number=@k
SET @OrigSpText3=(SELECT ctext FROM syscomments WHERE id=object_id(@objectname) and colid=@n and number=@k)
if @n=1
begin
if @type='P'
SET @OrigSpText2=(case when @number>1 then 'CREATE PROCEDURE '+ @objectname +';'+rtrim(@k)+' WITH ENCRYPTION AS '
                       else 'CREATE PROCEDURE '+ @objectname +' WITH ENCRYPTION AS '
                       end)
if @type='FN' or @type='TF' or @type='IF'
SET @OrigSpText2=(case @type when 'TF' then 
'CREATE FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns @b table(a varchar(10)) with encryption as begin insert @b select @a return end '
when 'FN' then
'CREATE FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns char(1) with encryption as begin return @a end'
when 'IF' then
'CREATE FUNCTION '+ @objectname+'(@a char(1)) returns table with encryption as return select @a as a'
end)
if @type='TR' 
begin
if @tr_parent_xtype='V'
begin
set @OrigSpText2='CREATE TRIGGER '+@objectname+' ON '+OBJECT_NAME(@parentid)+' WITH ENCRYPTION INSTEAD OF INSERT AS PRINT 1 '
end
else
begin
set @OrigSpText2='CREATE TRIGGER '+@objectname+' ON '+OBJECT_NAME(@parentid)+' WITH ENCRYPTION FOR INSERT AS PRINT 1 '
end
end
if @type='V'
set @OrigSpText2='CREATE VIEW '+@objectname+' WITH ENCRYPTION AS SELECT 1 as f'
set @q=4000-len(@OrigSpText2)
set @OrigSpText2=@OrigSpText2+REPLICATE('-',@q)
end
else
begin
SET @OrigSpText2=REPLICATE('-', 4000)
end
SET @i=1
SET @resultsp = replicate(N'A', (datalength(@OrigSpText1) / 2))
WHILE @i<=datalength(@OrigSpText1)/2
BEGIN
SET @resultsp = stuff(@resultsp, @i, 1, NCHAR(UNICODE(substring(@OrigSpText1, @i, 1)) ^
                                (UNICODE(substring(@OrigSpText2, @i, 1)) ^
                                UNICODE(substring(@OrigSpText3, @i, 1)))))
 SET @i=@i+1
END
set @orgvarbin=cast(@OrigSpText1 as varbinary(8000))
set @resultsp=(case when @encrypted=1 
                    then @resultsp 
                    else convert(nvarchar(4000),case when @status&2=2 then uncompress(@orgvarbin) else @orgvarbin end)
               end)
print @resultsp
set @n=@n+1
end
end
set @k=@k+1
end
drop table #temp
rollback tran
end


GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_GetSellLog]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSellLog]
	@createid	int,
	@uid	int,
	@cid	int
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @err int
set @err=0
if @createid<>''
begin
	select * from selllog where createid=@createid
	return @err
end
if @uid<>''
begin
	select * from selllog where uid=@uid
	return @err
end
if @cid<>''
begin
	select * from selllog where cid=@cid
	return @err
end
select * from selllog
return @err


GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_SellLog]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_SellLog]
	@createid		int,
	@uid		int,
	@cid		int,
	@itemid		varchar(50),
	@itemname	varchar(100), 
	@amount		varchar(50), 
	@point		int, 
	@price		smallmoney,
	@ip		varchar(15)
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @err int
declare @newtime smalldatetime;
SET @newtime = GETDATE();

set @err=0
insert SellLog
(createid, uid, cid, itemprototypeid, itemname, amount, point, price, itemin, ip)
values
(@createid, @uid, @cid, @itemid, @itemname, @amount, @point, @price, @newtime, @ip)
return @err

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[spselllog_count]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
--管理網頁http://www.youxiland.net/sys2/admin/list.asp取資料筆數.金額.點數.日數等合計資訊
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spselllog_count]
	@ptype1	varchar(20),
	@ptype2	varchar(10),
	@stime		varchar(12),
	@etime		varchar(12)
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
IF (@ptype2 <>'')
BEGIN
	SELECT  COUNT(*)  as log_count,sum([price]) as log_cash,sum([point]) as log_point
	FROM selllog
	WHERE createid=@ptype1 and itemin>=@stime and itemin<@etime and (price>0 or point>0)
end
else
BEGIN
	if (@ptype1 <>'')
	begin
		SELECT  COUNT(*)  as log_count,sum([price]) as log_cash,sum([point]) as log_point
		FROM selllog
		WHERE createid=@ptype1 and itemin>=@stime and itemin<@etime and (price>0 or point>0)
	end 
	else
	begin
		SELECT  COUNT(*)  as log_count,sum([price]) as log_cash,sum([point]) as log_point
		FROM selllog
		WHERE itemin>=@stime and itemin<@etime and (price>0 or point>0)
	end
end


GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[test]    Script Date: 4/23/2024 9:34:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[test] 
AS
DECLARE @err int
DECLARE @point int
DECLARE @price int
DECLARE @discount numeric(3,2)
DECLARE @today smalldatetime
set @today = getdate()
set @err = 0
select @point=point,@discount=discount, @point=point, @price=price  from SellItem where CreateID = 1
if @today > '2007/1/31 13:36:00' and @today < '2007/1/31 13:50:00'
begin
  select @point=@point*@discount,@price=@price*@discount
end
  select @today as today,@err as err,@point as point,@discount as discount,@price as price


GO
